 What is HTTP and HTTPS Simply put, the secure version of HTTP is HTTPS
 yahaan s kaa matlab sicyor he
 Data transferred between the browser and the websites that use HTTPS remains secure
 matlab ye he ki aapke or website ke bich kiye jane vaale sabhi communication encripted hote hai
 To check if a website uses HTTPS or not, look for the padlock icon before the URL in the left side of the web browser

 Encryption is of many levels, you can also check it by clicking on the padlock icon

 The practice of playing conch shells in worship is from ages to ages
 desh ke kai bhaagon main log shankh ko puujaghar main rakhte hai or ise niyamit rup se bajaate hai
 In such a situation, it is quite natural that the conch is only useful in worship or it has some direct benefit
 darasal, sanathan dharm kii kai aisi baaten hai, jo na keval aadhyatmik rup se, balki kai duusare tarah se bhi phydemand hai
 Conch shelling, ringing and proper use of its water has many benefits
 kai phaayde to sidhe taur par sehat se jude hai
 It is further discussed that what are the benefits of playing conch and its use in worship
 1
 It is believed that the house where there is a conch is inhabited by Lakshmi
 dharmik granthon main shankh ko lakshmi kaa bhai bataaya gaya he, kyonki lakshmi kii tarah shankh bhi sagar se hi utpann hua he
 The conch is counted among the fourteen gems derived from the churning of the sea
 2
 The conch is also considered auspicious because both Goddess Lakshmi and Lord Vishnu hold it in their hands
 3
 Playing conch shells in the ritual of worship makes the atmosphere pure
 jahaan tak isaki aawaaj jaati he, ise sunakar logon ke man main sakaaratmak vichaar paidaa hote hai
 The fruit of good thoughts is also naturally better
 4
 The anointing of Shiva, Lakshmi etc
 with the water of conch shell pleases God and gets his grace
 5
 The Brahmavaivarta Purana states that the atmosphere is purified by placing water in the conch and sprinkling it
 6
 The sound of the conch inspires people to worship
 aisi manyata he ki shankh kii puja se kamanaayen puri hoti hai
 This does not cause evil spirits to pass
 7
 Scientists believe that many kinds of bacteria and germs present in the atmosphere are destroyed by the sound of a conch shell
 kai test se is tarah ke nattejey mili hai
 8
 ayurveda ke mutabik, shankhodak ke bhasma ke upyog se pet kii bimaariyaan, pathari, pilia aadi kai tarah kii bimaariyaan dur hoti hai
 However, it should be used only on the advice of expert Vaidya
 9
 Playing the conch exercises the lungs
 puraanon ke zikr miltaa he ki agar shwaas kaa rogi niyamit taur par shankh bajaae, to vah beemaari se mukt ho saktaa he
 10
 shankh main rakhe pani kaa seven karne se haddiyaan majboot hoti hai
 It is also beneficial for teeth
 shankh main calcium, phosphorus va gandhak ke gun hone kii vajah se yah phydemand he
 11
 vaastushastra ke mutabik bhi shankh main aise kai gun hote hai, jisase ghar main positive energy aati he
